get a (pointer) value (explicit) 

Performs explicit type conversion between the JSON value and a compatible value if required.


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item If the requested type is a pointer to the internally stored JSON value that pointer is returned. No copies are made.
\item If the requested type is the current \doxylink{classbasic__json}{basic\+\_\+json}, or a different \doxylink{classbasic__json}{basic\+\_\+json} convertible from the current \doxylink{classbasic__json}{basic\+\_\+json}.
\item Otherwise the value is converted by calling the \doxylink{classbasic__json_ab75fd791f0b8fca724e5ed70b4956414}{json\+\_\+serializer$<$\+Value\+Type$>$} {\ttfamily from\+\_\+json()} method.
\end{DoxyItemize}


\begin{DoxyTemplParams}{Template Parameters}
{\em Value\+Type\+CV} & the provided value type \\
\hline
{\em Value\+Type} & the returned value type\\
\hline
\end{DoxyTemplParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
copy of the JSON value, converted to 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\begin{DoxyTemplParams}{Template Parameters}
{\em Value\+Type} & if necessary\\
\hline
\end{DoxyTemplParams}

\begin{DoxyExceptions}{Exceptions}
{\em what} & \doxylink{classbasic__json_ab75fd791f0b8fca724e5ed70b4956414}{json\+\_\+serializer$<$\+Value\+Type$>$} {\ttfamily from\+\_\+json()} method throws if conversion is required\\
\hline
\end{DoxyExceptions}
\begin{DoxySince}{Since}
version 2.\+1.\+0 
\end{DoxySince}

get a pointer value (explicit) 

Explicit pointer access to the internally stored JSON value. No copies are made.

\begin{DoxyWarning}{Warning}
The pointer becomes invalid if the underlying JSON object changes.
\end{DoxyWarning}

\begin{DoxyTemplParams}{Template Parameters}
{\em Pointer\+Type} & pointer type; must be a pointer to \doxylink{classbasic__json_a60644b7dccc409e6b367361d37841333}{array\+\_\+t}, \doxylink{classbasic__json_a67bb0d6dfaf1709d918b7107f5b94a3d}{object\+\_\+t}, \doxylink{classbasic__json_ac8c9cde32146e6c343e1960aefc11fba}{string\+\_\+t}, \doxylink{classbasic__json_a9301890c48e9b957edc07f9eb767bd10}{boolean\+\_\+t}, \doxylink{classbasic__json_aba48b0bdee31228a4e19b7c040b6d2a5}{number\+\_\+integer\+\_\+t}, \doxylink{classbasic__json_ae8505b599e706768a1e0bd6718cc7117}{number\+\_\+unsigned\+\_\+t}, or \doxylink{classbasic__json_a80a229dbc84c1334171ce9c49c873c56}{number\+\_\+float\+\_\+t}.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyTemplParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
pointer to the internally stored JSON value if the requested pointer type {\itshape Pointer\+Type} fits to the JSON value; {\ttfamily nullptr} otherwise
\end{DoxyReturn}
@complexity Constant.

@liveexample\{The example below shows how pointers to internal values of a JSON value can be requested. Note that no type conversions are made and a {\ttfamily nullptr} is returned if the value and the requested pointer type does not match.,get\+\_\+\+\_\+\+Pointer\+Type\}

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
see \doxylink{classbasic__json_aba60354728e2f7f64e3e5c6b02c5b820}{get\+\_\+ptr()} for explicit pointer-\/member access
\end{DoxySeeAlso}
\begin{DoxySince}{Since}
version 1.\+0.\+0 
\end{DoxySince}

template$<$typename Value\+Type , typename std\+::enable\+\_\+if$<$ \mbox{\hyperlink{structdetail_1_1conjunction}{detail\+::conjunction}}$<$ \mbox{\hyperlink{structdetail_1_1negation}{detail\+::negation}}$<$ std\+::is\+\_\+pointer$<$ Value\+Type $>$ $>$, \mbox{\hyperlink{structdetail_1_1negation}{detail\+::negation}}$<$ std\+::is\+\_\+same$<$ Value\+Type, std\+::nullptr\+\_\+t $>$ $>$, \mbox{\hyperlink{structdetail_1_1negation}{detail\+::negation}}$<$ std\+::is\+\_\+same$<$ Value\+Type, \mbox{\hyperlink{classdetail_1_1json__ref}{detail\+::json\+\_\+ref}}$<$ \mbox{\hyperlink{classbasic__json}{basic\+\_\+json}} $>$ $>$ $>$, \mbox{\hyperlink{structdetail_1_1negation}{detail\+::negation}}$<$ std\+::is\+\_\+same$<$ Value\+Type, typename string\+\_\+t\+::value\+\_\+type $>$ $>$, \mbox{\hyperlink{structdetail_1_1negation}{detail\+::negation}}$<$ \mbox{\hyperlink{structdetail_1_1is__basic__json}{detail\+::is\+\_\+basic\+\_\+json}}$<$ Value\+Type $>$ $>$, \mbox{\hyperlink{structdetail_1_1negation}{detail\+::negation}}$<$ std\+::is\+\_\+same$<$ Value\+Type, std\+::initializer\+\_\+list$<$ typename string\+\_\+t\+::value\+\_\+type $>$ $>$ $>$, \mbox{\hyperlink{structdetail_1_1is__detected__lazy}{detail\+::is\+\_\+detected\+\_\+lazy}}$<$ \mbox{\hyperlink{namespacedetail_afad0060784c2bfd69c62e4fd434ebcb8}{detail\+::get\+\_\+template\+\_\+function}}, const basic\+\_\+json\+\_\+t \&, Value\+Type $>$ $>$\mbox{\hyperlink{classbasic__json_a80c2436388fd16a1529ce9afce8229ef}{\+::value}}, int $>$\mbox{\hyperlink{classbasic__json_ac5e52dbb3cb4e9fcabd1b88c37985aef}{\+::type}}  = 0$>$ \\
\mbox{\hyperlink{json_8hpp_aefed8cf27cadeea45f12c6f3db3ce774}{JSON\+\_\+\+EXPLICIT}} \mbox{\hyperlink{classbasic__json}{basic\+\_\+json}}$<$ Object\+Type, Array\+Type, String\+Type, Boolean\+Type, Number\+Integer\+Type, Number\+Unsigned\+Type, Number\+Float\+Type, Allocator\+Type, JSONSerializer, Binary\+Type, Custom\+Base\+Class $>$\+::operator Value\+Type (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption}) const\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}



get a value (implicit) 

Implicit type conversion between the JSON value and a compatible value. The call is realized by calling \doxylink{classbasic__json_a0ab31c7fdbab38898070bca01637f886}{get() const}.


\begin{DoxyTemplParams}{Template Parameters}
{\em Value\+Type} & non-\/pointer type compatible to the JSON value, for instance {\ttfamily int} for JSON integer numbers, {\ttfamily bool} for JSON booleans, or {\ttfamily std\+::vector} types for JSON arrays. The character type of \doxylink{classbasic__json_ac8c9cde32146e6c343e1960aefc11fba}{string\+\_\+t} as well as an initializer list of this type is excluded to avoid ambiguities as these types implicitly convert to {\ttfamily std\+::string}.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyTemplParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
copy of the JSON value, converted to type {\itshape Value\+Type} 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\begin{DoxyExceptions}{Exceptions}
{\em type\+\_\+error.\+302} & in case passed type {\itshape Value\+Type} is incompatible to the JSON value type (e.\+g., the JSON value is of type boolean, but a string is requested); see example below\\
\hline
\end{DoxyExceptions}
@complexity Linear in the size of the JSON value.

@liveexample\{The example below shows several conversions from JSON values to other types. There a few things to note\+: (1) Floating-\/point numbers can be converted to integers\textbackslash{}, (2) A JSON array can be converted to a standard {\ttfamily std\+::vector\texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}short\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}}\textbackslash{}, (3) A JSON object can be converted to C++ associative containers such as {\ttfamily std\+::unordered\+\_\+map\texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}std\+::string\textbackslash{}, json\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}}.,operator\+\_\+\+\_\+\+Value\+Type\}

\begin{DoxySince}{Since}
version 1.\+0.\+0 
\end{DoxySince}

\begin{DoxyRefDesc}{Deprecated}
\item[\mbox{\hyperlink{deprecated__deprecated000004}{Deprecated}}]This stream operator is deprecated since 3.\+0.\+0 and will be removed in version 4.\+0.\+0 of the library. Please use \doxylink{classbasic__json_aea0de29387d532e0bc5f2475cb83995d}{operator$>$$>$(std\+::istream\&, basic\+\_\+json\&)} instead; that is, replace calls like {\ttfamily j \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}\texorpdfstring{$<$}{<} i;} with {\ttfamily i \texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>} j;}. \end{DoxyRefDesc}
